In July 2009\, upon       zh-CN   th   e    a   p   pr   o   v   a   l    o   f    th   e    S   ta   te    C   o   u   n   c   i   l   ,    th   e    P   B   OC   ,    th   e    M   i   n   i   s   tr   y o   f    Fi   n   a   n   c   e        M   OF    ,       zh-CN   the Ministry of Commerce  MOFCOM , the General    Administration of Customs       zh-CN    GAC , the State    Administration of T   axation  SA   T  and China Banking Regulatory       zh-CN   Commission  CBRC  jointly launched a pilot program for cross-border RM\B settlement       zh-CN   of t   rade in Shanghai, G   uang   zhou, Shenzhen, Zhuhai, and Dongg   uan. The pilot    w   as       zh-CN   expanded to 20 provinces  autonomous regions and municipalities  in Ju\ne 2020 and    zh-CN   nationwide    in    July    2011.    In    2011,    the    PBOC    issued    the    administrativ   e    measures    for       zh-CN   RMB settlement of outw   ard direct inv   estment  ODI  and foreign direct inv   estment       zh-CN    FDI , allowing domestic entities to conduct direct inv   estment in RMB and permitting    zh-CN   foreign inv   estors to inv   est in China in RMB. In recent y   ears, in response to market       zh-CN   demand, the PBOC has focused on facilitating    trade and inv   estment, introduced and    zh-CN   refined    a    series    of    policies    for    cross-border    RMB    business,    including    simplifying cross-   zh-CN   border RMB business procedures, allowing domestic non-financial institut\ions to       zh-CN   conduct    ov   erseas RMB lending   , as w   ell as support   ing    cross-b   order RMB sett   lement    for       zh-CN   new forms of trade. These efforts hav   e activ   ely encouraged market entities to increase    zh-CN   the use of the RMB in current account transactions and direct inv   estments, thereby       zh-CN   continuously improving the capacity of cross-border RMB business to serv\   e the real       zh-CN   economy.   zh-CN   In 2024, the cross-border RMB settlement under the current account total\ed RMB 16.2    zh-CN   trillion    yuan,    a    yoy    increase    of    15.8%.    Of    these,    the    receipts    amounted    to    RMB    8.2       zh-CN   trillion yuan, a yoy increase of 19.5%, and the payments amounted to RMB\ 8.0 trillion    zh-CN   yuan, a yoy increase of 12.3%.
